<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">accommodation</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">accommodātiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> accommodation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">lodging, facility</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> accommodation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">adaptation to circumstances</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">accordéon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Akkordion</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***acetaminophen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:acetaminophen.html>acetaminophen</a> (110052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of the chemical name para-acetylaminophenol.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:acetaminophen.html>acetaminophen</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">acetaminophens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Canada, US</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A white crystalline compound used in medicine as an anodyne to relieve pain and reduce fever.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:joel.html>Joel</a> Mabus (music),  “The Druggist”:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You need to take <b><a href = vnd.unilang:acetaminophen.html>acetaminophen</a></b> / Or just a little aspirin / acetylsalicylic for the pain</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paracetamol.html>paracetamol</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">para-acetylaminophenol</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tylenol.html>tylenol</a></span></li></ul>
</body>

***acht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a> (722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:achten.html>achte</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ahto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahtōu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*oḱtṓw</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_3">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>eight</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:achten.html>achte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ahta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahtō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>attention, heed</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-, second- and third-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achten.html>achten</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achten.html>achten</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b>[A] <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></b>

***achten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achten.html>achten</a> (9968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:achten.html>achten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ahton</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahtōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to esteem, to respect, to value</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to estimate, to consider, to reckon</li></ol>

***achtenveertig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achtenveertig.html>achtenveertig</a> (42655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veertig.html>veertig</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achtenveertig.html>achtenveertig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>forty-eight</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>

***achterbaks.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a> (21431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">achterbaecs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">behind one's back</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbakser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">achterbakst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shrewd, sneaky, underhand, furtive
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbakse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He really <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>sneaky</b> bastard.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Acting "<a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to act in a way you wouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> expect from well-behaved people, implied <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> little profit or benefit for the one doing it and big loss for the one it's done to.
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a></b>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:stiekem.html>stiekem</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbakse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:streek.html>streek</a>!</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***achterhalen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterhalen.html>achterhalen</a> (5971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">achter-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:halen.html>halen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterhalen.html>achterhalen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overtake, to hunt down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find out, discover</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">behind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kant.html>kant</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">side</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">behind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klappen.html>klappen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to talk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, literally “talk behind one's back”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterklap.html>achterklap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterklap.html>achterklapje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(mean-spirited) gossip
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> werksfeer <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verziekt.html>verziekt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:achterklap.html>achterklap</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:personeel.html>personeel</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The working environment <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> fouled by all the <b>gossipping</b> among the employees.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterom.html>achterom</a> (5208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterom.html>achterom</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>around the back
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> áchterom gekéken?</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Have you looked around the house yet?</dd></dl></li>
<li>backwards <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the shoulder
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> achterómgekeken?</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Have you looked <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> your shoulder yet?</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keek.html>keek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterom.html>achterom</a>.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> She looked back.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the first meaning the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a separate adverb of location, in the second a separable prepositional adverb that can be attached to certain verbs. Used as a preposition it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written in two parts:
</p>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>Achter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Around the back of the house.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>Loop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>!</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Come around the back!</dd></dl>
